***обод.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обод.html>о́бод</a> (26835)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*obvodъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обод.html>о́бод</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">óbod</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обод.html>о́бода</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обод.html>обо́дья</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обод.html>о́боды</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обод.html>обо́дьев</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обод.html>о́бодов</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ободок.html>ободо́к</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* Nonstandard.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>

***ободрать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ободрать.html>ободра́ть</a> (9402)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">обо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:драть.html>драть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ободрать.html>ободра́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obodrátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обдирать.html>обдира́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to strip, to peel, to skin, to flay, to flense
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ободрать.html>ободра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кора.html>кору́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>де́рева</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obodrátʹ</b> korú s déreva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bark a tree</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to scratch <i>(on)</i>, to scrape <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ободрать.html>ободра́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:об.html>об</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стена.html>сте́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obodrátʹ</b> rúku ob sténu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to scratch/scrape one's arm on a wall</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fleece, to rook
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ободрать.html>ободра́ть</a></b> кого́-нибудь <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:липка.html>ли́пку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>obodrátʹ</b> kovó-nibudʹ kak lípku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fleece someone; rob someone blind</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***обознаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обознаться.html>обозна́ться</a> (22871)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">обо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>знать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">znatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обознаться.html>обозна́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oboznátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">обознава́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to confuse one thing or person with another, to mistake, to not recognize
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извинить.html>извини́те</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:обознаться.html>обозна́лся</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приятель.html>прия́тель</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шапка.html>ша́пке</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Izviníte, ja <b>oboználsja</b>, u menjá prijátelʹ v takój že šápke.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'm sorry, I <b>confused you with someone else</b>; my friend has the same hat.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перепутать.html>перепу́тать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">perepútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спутать.html>спу́тать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">spútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принять.html>приня́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prinjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обозначать.html>обознача́ть</a> (7566)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обозначить.html>обозна́чить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oboznáčitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обозначить.html>обозна́ченный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oboznáčennyj</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:обозревать.html>обозрева́ть</a> (20768)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обозреть.html>обозре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obozrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обозревать.html>обозрева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">obozrevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обозреть.html>обозре́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to survey, to view, to look round</li>
<li>to review, to overview</li></ol>
